    <script type="text/javascript">
    $(function(){
        //set current module button style
        $("#nav_ask").attr('className',"on");
        $('#editor').TextAreaResizer();

        //toggle preview of editor
        //todo remove copy-paste
        var display = true;
        var txt = "[esconder preview]";
        $('#pre-collapse').text(txt);
        $('#pre-collapse').bind('click', function() {
            txt = display ? "[mostrar preview]" : "[esconder preview]";
            display = !display;
            $('#previewer').toggle();
            $('#pre-collapse').text(txt);
        });

        //Tags autocomplete action
        $("#id_tags").autocomplete("/tags_relacionadas/", {
            minChars: 1,
            matchContains: true,
            max: 10,
            multiple: true,
            multipleSeparator: " ",
            highlightItem: true,
            scroll: true,
            scrollHeight: 300,

            formatItem: function(row, i, max, value) {
                return row[1] + " (" + row[2] + ")";
            },

            formatResult: function(row, i, max, value) {
                return row[1];
            }
        });

    });

    function submitClicked(e, f) {
        if (!(browserTester('chrome') || browserTester('safari'))) {
            $("input.submit").disabled=true;
        }
        window.removeEventListener('beforeunload', beforeUnload, true);
        if (f) {
            f.submit();
        }
    }

    function beforeUnload(e) {
        if($("input#id_title")[0].value != "" || $("textarea#editor")[0].value != "" || $("input#id_tags")[0].value != "") {
            return yourWorkWillBeLost(e);
        }
    }
    window.addEventListener('beforeunload', beforeUnload, true);

      <script>
          function selecionaTipoConteudoParaBuscaTextual() {
              //zera o que estiver marcado
              $("#searchBar .options input[type=radio]").removeAttr("checked");
              var inputRadioId = "#type-" + $("#nav").find(".on").attr("id")

              if($(inputRadioId).length > 0){
                $(inputRadioId).attr("checked", true);
              } else {
                  //default perguntas
                $("#type-nav_questions").attr("checked", true);
              }
          }
          $(document).ready(function() {
            selecionaTipoConteudoParaBuscaTextual();
          });
      </script>

<div class="boxC" id="editor_side_bar">
    <p class="subtitle darkred primary-title">Markdown Básico</p>
    <ul class="list-item">
        <li>
            *italico* ou __italico__
        </li>
        <li>
			**negrito** or __negrito__
        </li>
        <li>
            <b>link</b>:[texto](http://url.com/ "Qual é a sua dúvida?")

        </li>

        <li>
            <b>imagem</b>?![alt texto](/path/img.jpg "Qual é a sua dúvida?")

        </li>
        <li>
			lista numerada:
            1.  Foo
            2.  Bar
        </li>
        <li>
			para adicionar uma quebra de linha basta adicionar dois espaços onde você gostaria que a nova linha estivesse.
        </li>
        <li>
			tags HTML básicas também são suportadas
        </li>
    </ul>
    <p class='info-box-follow-up-links'>
        <a href="/ajuda_markdown/" target="_blank">aprenda mais sobre Markdown </a>

(function() {
    'use strict';

    var timerId ; // Current timer handler
    var refreshTime = 300000; // 1000*60*5
    var graceTimerStep = 10000; // 1000*10

    var isMobile = function() {
        return ($('#regua-navegacao:visible').length > 0);
    };

    var preparePlayer = function(player) {

        var refreshPageWithTimeout = function() {

            console.log('Trying to refresh on' + graceTimerStep + ' ms.');
            setTimeout(function() {
                    if (!player.isPlaying()) {
                        refreshPage();
                    }
                    console.log('Watching a video. Refresh the page later');
                }, graceTimerStep);
        };

        var playerComplete = player.complete;
        if ($.isFunction(playerComplete)) {
            player.complete = function() {
                playerComplete.apply(this, arguments);
                refreshPage();
            };
        }
        else {
            player.complete = refreshPage;
        }

        var playerOnPause = player.onPause;
        if ($.isFunction(playerOnPause)) {
            player.onPause = function() {
                playerOnPause.apply(this, arguments);
                refreshPageWithTimeout(player);
            };
        }
        else {
            player.onPause = refreshPageWithTimeout;
        }

        var playerOnStop = player.onStop;
        if ($.isFunction(playerOnStop)) {
            player.onStop = function() {
              playerOnStop.apply(this, arguments);
              refreshPageWithTimeout();
          };
        }
        else {
            player.onStop = refreshPageWithTimeout;
        }
    };

    var refreshPage = function() {
        if (!isMobile()) {
            console.log('Refreshing now');
            window.location.reload();
        }
        else {
            console.log('Is mobile: Not reloading the page.');
        }
    };

    var checkForVideoPlaying = function() {

        console.log('Timeout: Refreshing the page at any moment.');

        clearTimeout(timerId); // clear timer

        var isVideoPlaying = false;

        $.each(WM.PlayerManager, function(index, player) {
            isVideoPlaying = isVideoPlaying || player.isPlaying();
            if (player.isPlaying()) {
                preparePlayer(player);
            }
        });

        if (!isVideoPlaying) {
            refreshPage();
        }

    };

    var startTimer = function() {
        timerId = setTimeout(checkForVideoPlaying, refreshTime);
    };

    $(document).ready(function() {
        if (!isMobile() && window.location.hash != '#debug' ) {
            console.log('Time Started: ' + refreshTime + ' ms until Refresh.');
            startTimer();
        }
    });

})();
</script></body><!-- Página gerada em 28/03/2017 13:12:37 --></html>
